agot_schedule_scripted_hair_update_effect = {
	save_scope_as = hair_victim
	save_scope_value_as = {
		name = scripted_hair
		value = flag:$HAIR$
	}
	save_scope_value_as = {
		name = scripted_appearance_update_age
		value = $AGE$
	}
	if = {
		limit = { agot_scripted_appearance_update_years >= 0 }
		trigger_event = {
			id = agot_appearance_events.9000
			years = agot_scripted_appearance_update_years
		}
	}
	else = {
		agot_update_scripted_hair_effect = yes
	}
}

agot_schedule_scripted_beard_update_effect = {
	save_scope_as = hair_victim
	save_scope_value_as = {
		name = scripted_beard
		value = flag:$BEARD$
	}
	save_scope_value_as = {
		name = scripted_appearance_update_age
		value = $AGE$
	}
	if = {
		limit = { agot_scripted_appearance_update_years >= 0 }
		trigger_event = {
			id = agot_appearance_events.9001
			years = agot_scripted_appearance_update_years
		}
	}
	else = {
		agot_update_scripted_beard_effect = yes
	}
}

agot_update_scripted_beard_effect = {
	agot_remove_scripted_beard_effect = yes
	if = {
		limit = { is_alive = yes }

		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:scripted_beard ?= flag:beard_trait_no_beard
			}
			add_character_flag = beard_trait_no_beard
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:scripted_beard ?= flag:beard_trait_male_beard_western_01
			}
			add_character_flag = beard_trait_male_beard_western_01
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:scripted_beard ?= flag:beard_trait_male_beard_western_02
			}
			add_character_flag = beard_trait_male_beard_western_02
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:scripted_beard ?= flag:beard_trait_male_beard_western_03
			}
			add_character_flag = beard_trait_male_beard_western_03
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:scripted_beard ?= flag:beard_trait_male_beard_western_04
			}
			add_character_flag = beard_trait_male_beard_western_04
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:scripted_beard ?= flag:beard_trait_male_beard_western_05
			}
			add_character_flag = beard_trait_male_beard_western_05
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:scripted_beard ?= flag:beard_trait_male_beard_western_06
			}
			add_character_flag = beard_trait_male_beard_western_06
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:scripted_beard ?= flag:beard_trait_male_beard_western_07
			}
			add_character_flag = beard_trait_male_beard_western_07
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:scripted_beard ?= flag:beard_trait_male_beard_western_08
			}
			add_character_flag = beard_trait_male_beard_western_08
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:scripted_beard ?= flag:beard_trait_male_beard_western_09
			}
			add_character_flag = beard_trait_male_beard_western_09
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:scripted_beard ?= flag:beard_trait_male_beard_western_10
			}
			add_character_flag = beard_trait_male_beard_western_10
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:scripted_beard ?= flag:beard_trait_male_beard_mena_01
			}
			add_character_flag = beard_trait_male_beard_mena_01
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:scripted_beard ?= flag:beard_trait_male_beard_mena_02
			}
			add_character_flag = beard_trait_male_beard_mena_02
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:scripted_beard ?= flag:beard_trait_male_beard_mena_03
			}
			add_character_flag = beard_trait_male_beard_mena_03
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:scripted_beard ?= flag:beard_trait_male_beard_mena_04
			}
			add_character_flag = beard_trait_male_beard_mena_04
		}

		remove_trait = beard_trait_male_agot_old_king_beard_01
	}
}

agot_schedule_scripted_hair_dye_update_effect = {
	save_scope_as = hair_victim
	save_scope_value_as = {
		name = scripted_hair_dye
		value = flag:$DYE$
	}
	save_scope_value_as = {
		name = scripted_appearance_update_age
		value = $AGE$
	}
	if = {
		limit = { agot_scripted_appearance_update_years >= 0 }
		trigger_event = {
			id = agot_appearance_events.9002
			years = agot_scripted_appearance_update_years
		}
	}
	else = {
		agot_update_scripted_hair_dye_effect = yes
	}
}

agot_update_scripted_hair_dye_effect = {
	agot_remove_scripted_hair_dye_effect = yes
	if = {
		limit = { is_alive = yes }
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:scripted_hair_dye ?= flag:poppy_hair_dye
			}
			add_character_modifier = poppy_hair_dye
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				scope:scripted_hair_dye ?= flag:asshaii_scarlet_hair_dye
			}
			add_character_modifier = asshaii_scarlet_hair_dye
		}

			limit = {

agot_hair_dye_death_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_character_modifier = poppy_hair_dye }
		make_trait_inactive = poppy_hair_dye
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_character_modifier = asshaii_scarlet_hair_dye }
		make_trait_inactive = asshaii_scarlet_hair_dye

agot_culture_appropiate_hair_dye_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			culture = culture:braavosi
		}
		agot_dark_hair_dye_effect = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			culture = culture:lyseni
		}
		agot_pastel_hair_dye_effect = yes
	}
	else = {
		agot_random_hair_dye_effect = yes
	}
}

agot_remove_heterochromia_eyes_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_inactive_trait = heterochromia_green1
		}
		make_trait_active = heterochromia_green1
		remove_trait = heterochromia_green1
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_inactive_trait = heterochromia_green2
		}
		make_trait_active = heterochromia_green2
		remove_trait = heterochromia_green2
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_inactive_trait = heterochromia_blue1

agot_random_one_eyed_fashion_effect = {
	agot_remove_eye_gem_effect = yes
	agot_clear_eye_patch_flags_effect = yes
	random_list = {
		10 = {
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				is_lowborn = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				is_landless_adventurer = yes
			}

			add_character_flag = beric_eyepatch
		}
		10 = {
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				is_lowborn = yes
			}
			add_character_flag = eye_bandage_clean
		}
		10 = {
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						highest_held_title_tier >= tier_county
						is_landless_adventurer = no
					}
					any_close_family_member = {
						even_if_dead = yes
						highest_held_title_tier >= tier_county
						is_landless_adventurer = no
					}
				}
				NOR = {
					government_has_flag = government_is_pirate
					government_has_flag = government_is_tribal
					culture = { agot_is_wildling_culture = yes }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				OR = {
					AND = {
						highest_held_title_tier >= tier_kingdom
						is_landless_adventurer = no
					}
					any_close_family_member = {
						even_if_dead = yes
						highest_held_title_tier >= tier_kingdom
						is_landless_adventurer = no
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				OR = {
					AND = {
						highest_held_title_tier >= tier_empire
						is_landless_adventurer = no
					}
					any_close_family_member = {
						even_if_dead = yes
						highest_held_title_tier >= tier_empire
						is_landless_adventurer = no
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 200
				has_trait = fashionable
			}

			add_character_flag = decorated_eyepatch
		}
		10 = {
			add_character_flag = standard_eyepatch
		}
		10 = {
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				government_has_flag = government_is_pirate
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				culture = { has_cultural_pillar = heritage_ironman }
			}

			add_character_flag = round_eyepatch
		}
		10 = {
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				culture = { has_cultural_pillar = heritage_first_man }
			}

			add_character_flag = triangle_eyepatch
		}
		50 = {
			trigger = {
				OR = {
					government_has_flag = government_is_pirate
					AND = {
						government_has_flag = government_is_feudal
						OR = {
							AND = {
								highest_held_title_tier >= tier_kingdom
								is_landless_adventurer = no
							}
							any_close_family_member = {
								even_if_dead = yes
								highest_held_title_tier >= tier_kingdom
								is_landless_adventurer = no
							}
						}
					}
					AND = {
						government_has_flag = government_is_free_city
						OR = {
							AND = {
								highest_held_title_tier >= tier_duchy
								is_landless_adventurer = no
							}
							any_close_family_member = {
								even_if_dead = yes
								highest_held_title_tier >= tier_duchy
								is_landless_adventurer = no
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				short_term_gold >= 500
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				government_has_flag = government_is_free_city
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				OR = {
					AND = {
						highest_held_title_tier >= tier_kingdom
						is_landless_adventurer = no
					}
					any_close_family_member = {
						even_if_dead = yes
						highest_held_title_tier >= tier_kingdom
						is_landless_adventurer = no
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				OR = {
					AND = {
						highest_held_title_tier >= tier_empire
						is_landless_adventurer = no
					}
					any_close_family_member = {
						even_if_dead = yes
						highest_held_title_tier >= tier_empire
						is_landless_adventurer = no
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 200
				has_trait = arrogant
			}

			random_list = {
				1 = { add_character_flag = eye_gem_red }
				1 = { add_character_flag = eye_gem_blue }
				1 = { add_character_flag = eye_gem_white }
				1 = { add_character_flag = eye_gem_dark_blue }
				1 = { add_character_flag = eye_gem_green }
				1 = { add_character_flag = eye_gem_black }
				1 = { add_character_flag = eye_gem_yellow }
				1 = { add_character_flag = eye_gem_orange }
				1 = { add_character_flag = eye_gem_purple }
			}
		}
		10 = {
			trigger = {
				ai_boldness >= very_high_positive_ai_value
				NOT = { has_trait = fashionable }
			}

			add_character_flag = no_eyepatch
		}
	}
}

agot_random_visible_disfigurement_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_trait = disfigured
			NOR = {
				agot_has_visible_disfigurement_trigger = yes
				has_character_flag = is_Blackfyre_14
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			1 = { make_trait_inactive = visible_disfigurement_1 }
			1 = { make_trait_inactive = visible_disfigurement_2 }
			1 = { make_trait_inactive = visible_disfigurement_3 }
			1 = { make_trait_inactive = visible_disfigurement_4 }
			1 = { make_trait_inactive = visible_disfigurement_5 }
		}
	}
}

agot_remove_visible_disfigurement_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_inactive_trait = visible_disfigurement_1
		}
		make_trait_active = visible_disfigurement_1
		remove_trait = visible_disfigurement_1
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_inactive_trait = visible_disfigurement_2

		remove_trait = visible_disfigurement_2
	}
	if = {

			has_inactive_trait = visible_disfigurement_3
		}
		make_trait_active = visible_disfigurement_3
		remove_trait = visible_disfigurement_3
	}
	if = {

			has_inactive_trait = visible_disfigurement_4
		}
		make_trait_active = visible_disfigurement_4
		remove_trait = visible_disfigurement_4
	}
	if = {

		remove_trait = visible_disfigurement_5
	}
}

agot_visible_disfigurement_death_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_character_modifier = wearing_disfigurement_mask_modifier
			NOT = { has_character_flag = disfigurement_fully_masked }
		}
		make_trait_inactive = disfigurement_partially_masked
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_character_modifier = wearing_disfigurement_mask_modifier
			has_character_flag = disfigurement_fully_masked
		}
		make_trait_inactive = disfigurement_fully_masked
	}
}
